▶ Ledger Information (Show SQL & info) (export to excel)
Item NameItem Value
SQL
select a.target_ledger_id ledger_id, a.target_ledger_name name,
       b.currency_code currency_code,
       b.sla_accounting_method_code SLAM, a.target_ledger_category_code type
from   gl_ledger_relationships a,
       gl_ledgers b
where  a.primary_ledger_id = (select set_of_books_id
                              from   ar_cash_receipts_all
                              where  cash_receipt_id = 1611973)
and    a.primary_ledger_id = b.ledger_id

▶ SLAM for Primary Ledger (Show SQL & info) (export to excel)
Item NameItem Value
SQL
SELECT accounting_method_code SLAM_code, amb_context_code,
       substr(rpad(ACCOUNTING_METHOD_TYPE_CODE,8,' '),1,8) SLAM_type,
       product_rule_code AAD_code,
       product_rule_name AAD_name,
       substr(rpad(product_rule_type_code,8,' '),1,8) AAD_type,
       to_char(last_update_date, 'YYYY-MON-DD HH24:MI:SS')  last_update_date,
       to_char(creation_date, 'YYYY-MON-DD HH24:MI:SS')  creation_date ,
       to_char(start_date_active, 'YYYY-MON-DD')  start_date,
       to_char(end_date_active,'YYYY-MON-DD') end_date,
       application_id app_id,
       last_updated_by,
       created_by
FROM    xla_acctg_method_rules_fvl
where   application_id = 222
and    accounting_method_code IN
          (select sla_accounting_method_code
           from   gl_ledgers
           where  ledger_id = (select set_of_books_id
                               from   ar_cash_receipts_all
                               where  cash_receipt_id = 1611973)
          )
SLAM_CODE AMB_CONTEXT_CODE SLAM_TYPE AAD_CODE AAD_NAME AAD_TYPE LAST_UPDATE_DATE CREATION_DATE START_DATE END_DATE APP_ID LAST_UPDATED_BY CREATED_BY
OBA_STANDARD_ACCRUAL DEFAULT C AR_DEFAULT_ACCRUAL Receivables Default Accrual S 2013-OCT-11 11:54:47 2013-OCT-11 11:54:47 2000-JAN-01 222 1130 1130

▶ AAD for Primary Ledger (Show SQL & info) (export to excel)
Item NameItem Value
SQL
select PRODUCT_RULE_CODE,
       name ,
       to_char(creation_date, 'DD-MON-YYYY HH24:MI:SS') creation_date ,
       to_char(last_update_date, 'DD-MON-YYYY HH24:MI:SS') last_update,
           decode(COMPILE_STATUS_CODE,'Y','Compiled',
                                      'N','Not Compiled',
                                      'I','Invalid',
                                      'R','Validating',
                                     'Invalid - '||COMPILE_STATUS_CODE) STATUS_CODE,
      'XLA_00222_AAD_'||product_rule_type_code||'_00000'||product_rule_hash_id||'_PKG' AAD_Package,
      PRODUCT_RULE_HASH_ID,
      enabled_flag
      PRODUCT_RULE_TYPE_CODE,
      created_by,
      last_updated_by
from   xla_product_rules_fvl
where  application_id = 222
and    (PRODUCT_RULE_CODE, amb_context_code) in
                (SELECT PRODUCT_RULE_CODE, amb_context_code
                 FROM xla_acctg_method_rules_fvl
                 WHERE upper(application_name)='RECEIVABLES'
                 and   amb_context_code = 'DEFAULT'
                 and   accounting_method_code IN
                 (select sla_accounting_method_code
                  from gl_ledgers
                  where ledger_id = (select set_of_books_id
                                     from   ar_cash_receipts_all
                                     where  cash_receipt_id = 1611973)
          ))
PRODUCT_RULE_CODE NAME CREATION_DATE LAST_UPDATE STATUS_CODE AAD_PACKAGE PRODUCT_RULE_HASH_ID PRODUCT_RULE_TYPE_CODE CREATED_BY LAST_UPDATED_BY

SELECT a.filename, b.version,
to_char(b.creation_date,'YYYY/MM/DD') applied_date
FROM ad_files a,
ad_file_versions b
WHERE a.file_id = b.file_id
AND a.subdir = 'patch/115/import/US'
AND a.filename = 'ARXLAAAD.ldt'
ORDER BY 3 desc

▶ Receipt Class (Show SQL & info) (export to excel)
Item NameItem Value
SQL
SELECT  a.receipt_class_id receipt_class_id,
        a.name Name,
        a.notes_receivable Notes_Receivable,
        a.creation_method_code Creation_Method,
        a.confirm_flag Require_Confirmation,
        a.remit_method_code Remittance_Method,
        a.bill_of_exchange_flag Bill_of_Exchange,
        a.clear_flag Clearance_Method,
        a.remit_flag Remit_Flag,
        a.creation_status Creation_Status
FROM    AR_RECEIPT_CLASSES a,
        AR_RECEIPT_METHODS b,
        AR_CASH_RECEIPTS_ALL c
WHERE   b.receipt_class_id = a.receipt_class_id
AND     b.receipt_method_id = c.receipt_method_id
AND     c.cash_receipt_id = 1611973
RECEIPT_CLASS_ID NAME NOTES_RECEIVABLE CREATION_METHOD REQUIRE_CONFIRMATION REMITTANCE_METHOD BILL_OF_EXCHANGE CLEARANCE_METHOD REMIT_FLAG CREATION_STATUS

▶ Payment Method (Show SQL & info) (export to excel)
Item NameItem Value
SQL
SELECT  a.receipt_method_id Receipt_Method_Id,
        a.receipt_class_id  Receipt_Class_Id,
        a.name Name,
        a.printed_name Printed_Name,
        to_char(a.start_date,'DD-MON-YYYY') Effective_From_Date,
        to_char(a.end_date, 'DD-MON-YYYY')  Effective_To_Date,
        a.dm_inherit_receipt_num_flag Debit_Memos_Inherit_Rec_Number,
        a.receipt_inherit_inv_num_flag Receipts_Inherit_Trx_Numbers,
        a.receipt_creation_rule_code Number_of_Receipts_Rule,
        a.maturity_date_rule_code Receipt_Maturity_Date_Rule,
        a.auto_print_program_id Automatic_Print_Program,
        a.payment_type_code Payment_Type,
        a.lead_days Lead_Days
FROM    AR_RECEIPT_METHODS a,
        AR_CASH_RECEIPTS_ALL b
WHERE   a.receipt_method_id = b.receipt_method_id
AND     b.cash_receipt_id = 1611973

SELECT   a.receipt_method_id,
         a.remit_bank_acct_use_id,
         a.org_id,
         a.cash_ccid,
         a.on_account_ccid,
         a.unapplied_ccid,
         a.unidentified_ccid,
         a.bank_charges_ccid,
         a.factor_ccid,
         a.receipt_clearing_ccid,
         a.remittance_ccid,
         a.short_term_debt_ccid,
         a.edisc_receivables_trx_id,
         a.unedisc_receivables_trx_id
FROM     AR_RECEIPT_METHOD_ACCOUNTS_ALL a,
         AR_CASH_RECEIPTS_ALL b
WHERE    a.remit_bank_acct_use_id = b.remit_bank_acct_use_id
AND      a.receipt_method_id = b.receipt_method_id
AND      a.org_id = b.org_id
AND      b.cash_receipt_id = 1611973

▶ Receipt Status (Show SQL & info) (export to excel)
Item NameItem Value
SQL
select cash_receipt_history_id, cash_receipt_id, status
from   ar_cash_receipt_history_all
where  cash_receipt_id = 1611973
and    current_record_flag = 'Y'
and    status not in ('CLEARED', 'REVERSED')

SELECT   cash_receipt_history_id,
         status,
         to_char(gl_date, 'DD-MON-YYYY')    gl_date,
         sum(amount_applied),
         sum(amount_applied_from),
         sum(acctd_amount_applied_from),
         sum(acctd_amount_applied_to),
         sum(line_applied),
         sum(tax_applied),
         sum(freight_applied),
         sum(receivables_charges_applied),
         sum(earned_discount_taken),
         sum(unearned_discount_taken),
         sum(acctd_earned_discount_taken),
         sum(acctd_unearned_discount_taken)
FROM     AR_RECEIVABLE_APPLICATIONS_ALL
WHERE    cash_receipt_id = 1611973
GROUP BY cash_receipt_history_id, status, gl_date
ORDER BY gl_date

▶ AR_DISTRIBUTIONS_ALL Totals (Show SQL & info) (export to excel)
Item NameItem Value
SQL
SELECT dis.source_table,
       sum(dis.amount_dr),
       sum(dis.amount_cr),
       sum(dis.acctd_amount_dr),
       sum(dis.acctd_amount_cr),
       sum(dis.from_amount_dr),
       sum(dis.from_amount_cr),
       sum(dis.from_acctd_amount_dr),
       sum(dis.from_acctd_amount_cr)
FROM   AR_DISTRIBUTIONS_ALL dis,
       AR_CASH_RECEIPT_HISTORY_ALL crh
WHERE  crh.cash_receipt_id = 1611973
AND    dis.source_table = 'CRH'
AND    dis.source_id = crh.cash_receipt_history_id
GROUP BY dis.source_table
UNION
SELECT dis.source_table,
       sum(dis.amount_dr),
       sum(dis.amount_cr),
       sum(dis.acctd_amount_dr),
       sum(dis.acctd_amount_cr),
       sum(dis.from_amount_dr),
       sum(dis.from_amount_cr),
       sum(dis.from_acctd_amount_dr),
       sum(dis.from_acctd_amount_cr)
FROM   AR_DISTRIBUTIONS_ALL dis,
       AR_RECEIVABLE_APPLICATIONS_ALL ra
WHERE  ra.cash_receipt_id = 1611973
AND    dis.source_table = 'RA'
AND    dis.source_id = ra.receivable_application_id
GROUP BY dis.source_table
UNION
SELECT dis.source_table,
       sum(dis.amount_dr),
       sum(dis.amount_cr),
       sum(dis.acctd_amount_dr),
       sum(dis.acctd_amount_cr),
       sum(dis.from_amount_dr),
       sum(dis.from_amount_cr),
       sum(dis.from_acctd_amount_dr),
       sum(dis.from_acctd_amount_cr)
FROM   AR_DISTRIBUTIONS_ALL dis,
       AR_MISC_CASH_DISTRIBUTIONS_ALL mcd
WHERE  mcd.cash_receipt_id = 1611973
AND    dis.source_table = 'MCD'
AND    dis.source_id = mcd.misc_cash_distribution_id
GROUP BY dis.source_table
SOURCE_TABLE SUM(DIS.AMOUNT_DR) SUM(DIS.AMOUNT_CR) SUM(DIS.ACCTD_AMOUNT_DR) SUM(DIS.ACCTD_AMOUNT_CR) SUM(DIS.FROM_AMOUNT_DR) SUM(DIS.FROM_AMOUNT_CR) SUM(DIS.FROM_ACCTD_AMOUNT_DR) SUM(DIS.FROM_ACCTD_AMOUNT_CR)

▶ XLA Accounts (Show SQL & info) (export to excel)
Item NameItem Value
SQL
SELECT code_combination_id, concatenated_segments account,
       gl_control_account control_account,
       enabled_flag enabled,
       detail_posting_allowed detail_posting, alternate_code_combination_id,
       start_date_active start_date,
       end_date_active end_date
from   gl_code_combinations_kfv
where  code_combination_id in (select distinct code_combination_id
                               from   xla_ae_lines
                               WHERE  ae_header_id in (select ae_header_id
                                                       from   xla_ae_headers
                                                       where  application_id = 222
                                                       and    entity_id in (SELECT entity_id
                                                                            FROM   xla.xla_transaction_entities xte
                                                                            WHERE  xte.application_id = 222
                                                                            AND    xte.entity_code in ('RECEIPTS','MANUAL')
                                                                            and    nvl(source_id_int_1,-99) = 1611973)))

                        from   xla_ae_headers

                                             WHERE  xte.application_id = 222

                          )

▶ GL_JE_HEADERS (Show SQL & info) (export to excel)
Item NameItem Value
SQL
SELECT DISTINCT gjh.*
FROM   gl_je_headers gjh,
       gl_import_references gir,
       xla_ae_lines xal,
       xla_ae_headers xah
WHERE  gjh.je_header_id = gir.je_header_id
AND    gir.gl_sl_link_id = xal.gl_sl_link_id
AND    gir.gl_sl_link_table = xal.gl_sl_link_table
AND    xal.application_id = xah.application_id
AND    xal.ae_header_id = xah.ae_header_id
AND    xah.application_id = 222
AND    xah.entity_id IN (select xte.entity_id
                         from   xla.xla_transaction_entities xte
                         where  xte.entity_code in ('RECEIPTS','MANUAL')
                         and    xte.application_id  = 222
                         and    xte.source_id_int_1 = 1611973)

▶ GL_JE_LINES (Show SQL & info) (export to excel)
Item NameItem Value
SQL
SELECT   distinct gjl.*
FROM     GL_JE_LINES gjl, GL_IMPORT_REFERENCES gir,
         XLA_AE_LINES xal, xla_ae_headers xah
WHERE    gjl.je_header_id     = gir.je_header_id
AND      gjl.je_line_num      = gir.je_line_num
AND      gir.gl_sl_link_id    = xal.gl_sl_link_id
AND      gir.gl_sl_link_table = xal.gl_sl_link_table
AND      xal.application_id   = xah.application_id
AND      xal.ae_header_id     = xah.ae_header_id
AND      xah.application_id   = 222
AND      xah.entity_id IN (select xte.entity_id
                           from   xla.xla_transaction_entities xte
                           where  xte.entity_code in ('RECEIPTS','MANUAL')
                           and    xte.application_id  = 222
                           and    xte.source_id_int_1 = 1611973)

SELECT   distinct gir.*
FROM     GL_IMPORT_REFERENCES gir, XLA_AE_LINES xal,
         xla_ae_headers xah
WHERE    gir.gl_sl_link_id    = xal.gl_sl_link_id
AND      gir.gl_sl_link_table = xal.gl_sl_link_table
AND      xal.application_id   = xah.application_id
AND      xal.ae_header_id     = xah.ae_header_id
AND      xah.application_id   = 222
AND      xah.entity_id IN (select xte.entity_id
                           from   xla.xla_transaction_entities xte
                           where  xte.entity_code in ('RECEIPTS','MANUAL')
                           and    xte.application_id  = 222
                           and    xte.source_id_int_1 = 1611973)

SELECT    distinct gps.*
FROM      GL_PERIOD_STATUSES gps,
          AR_SYSTEM_PARAMETERS_ALL sys,
(SELECT   distinct gl_date
 FROM     AR_CASH_RECEIPT_HISTORY_ALL
 WHERE    cash_receipt_id = 1611973
 UNION
 SELECT   distinct gl_date
 FROM     AR_RECEIVABLE_APPLICATIONS_ALL
 WHERE    cash_receipt_id = 1611973
 UNION
 SELECT   distinct gl_date
 FROM     AR_MISC_CASH_DISTRIBUTIONS_ALL
 WHERE    cash_receipt_id = 1611973) atg_date
WHERE    atg_date.gl_date between gps.start_date and gps.end_date
AND      gps.application_id = 222
AND      NVL(sys.org_id, -99) = (select org_id
                                 from   ar_cash_receipts_all
                                 where  cash_receipt_id = 1611973)
AND      gps.set_of_books_id = sys.set_of_books_id
ORDER BY gps.period_name

▶ AR Forms, Libraries and Reports Versions (Show SQL & info) (export to excel)
Item NameItem Value
SQL
select b.filename, a.version, a.creation_date, b.subdir
from   ad_file_versions a, ad_files b
where  b.file_id = a.file_id
and    b.app_short_name = 'AR'
and    b.filename like '%.rdf'
and    a.creation_date = (select max(c.creation_date)
                          from   ad_file_versions c
                          where   c.file_id = a.file_id)
union
select b.filename, a.version, a.creation_date, b.subdir
from   ad_file_versions a, ad_files b
where  b.file_id = a.file_id
and    b.app_short_name = 'AR'
and    b.filename like '%.pll'
and    a.creation_date = (select max(c.creation_date)
                          from   ad_file_versions c
                          where  c.file_id = a.file_id)
union
select b.filename, a.version, a.creation_date, b.subdir
from   ad_file_versions a, ad_files b
where  b.file_id = a.file_id
and    b.app_short_name = 'AR'
and    b.filename like '%.fmb'
and    a.creation_date = (select max(c.creation_date)
                          from   ad_file_versions c
                          where   c.file_id = a.file_id)
order by 1
FILENAME VERSION CREATION_DATE SUBDIR

SELECT name, text, type
FROM   dba_source
where  ((name like 'AR%')
         or (name like 'RA%'))
and    line = 2
and    type in ('PACKAGE', 'PACKAGE BODY')

▶ AR Invalid PL/SQL Packages (Show SQL & info) (export to excel)
Item NameItem Value
SQL
SELECT a.object_name,
           decode(a.object_type,
             'PACKAGE', 'Package Spec',
             'PACKAGE BODY', 'Package Body',
             a.object_type) type,
           (
             SELECT ltrim(rtrim(substr(substr(c.text, instr(c.text,'Header: ')),
               instr(substr(c.text, instr(c.text,'Header: ')), ' ', 1, 1),
               instr(substr(c.text, instr(c.text,'Header: ')), ' ', 1, 2) -
               instr(substr(c.text, instr(c.text,'Header: ')), ' ', 1, 1)
               ))) || ' - ' ||
               ltrim(rtrim(substr(substr(c.text, instr(c.text,'Header: ')),
               instr(substr(c.text, instr(c.text,'Header: ')), ' ', 1, 2),
               instr(substr(c.text, instr(c.text,'Header: ')), ' ', 1, 3) -
               instr(substr(c.text, instr(c.text,'Header: ')), ' ', 1, 2)
               )))
             FROM dba_source c
             WHERE c.owner = a.owner
             AND   c.name = a.object_name
             AND   c.type = a.object_type
             AND   c.line = 2
             AND   c.text like '%$Header%'
           ) "File Version",
           b.text "Error Text"
    FROM dba_objects a,
         dba_errors b
    WHERE a.object_name = b.name(+)
    AND a.object_type = b.type(+)
    AND a.owner = 'APPS'
    AND (a.object_name like 'AR%')
    AND a.status = 'INVALID'
OBJECT_NAME TYPE File Version Error Text
0 rows selected - Elapsed time: .015 Sec

All checks passed.
There are no invalid objects for Receivables in the database.

               instr(substr(c.text, instr(c.text,'Header: ')), ' ', 1, 1)
